\DoxyCodeLine{3760   \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} newPreallocSize = minimumPreallocSize;}

\DoxyCodeLine{3764   ++mPreallocIteration;}

\DoxyCodeLine{3768   std::copy\_backward(mData.begin() + mPreallocSize,}
\DoxyCodeLine{3769                      mData.end() -\/ sizeDifference, mData.end());}
\DoxyCodeLine{3770   mPreallocSize = newPreallocSize;}

\DoxyCodeLine{3800         postAllocSize >}
\DoxyCodeLine{3801         usedSize * 1.5;  \textcolor{comment}{// QVector grow strategy is 2\string^n for static data. Watch}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3802                          \textcolor{comment}{// out not to oscillate!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3803     shrinkPreAllocation = mPreallocSize * 10 > usedSize;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3804   \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (totalAlloc >}
\DoxyCodeLine{3805              1000)  \textcolor{comment}{// below 10 MiB raw data be generous with preallocated}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3806                     \textcolor{comment}{// memory, below 1k points don't even bother}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3807   \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3808     shrinkPostAllocation = postAllocSize > usedSize * 5;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3809     shrinkPreAllocation =}

\DoxyCodeLine{3811                                          \textcolor{comment}{// postallocation, so can be smaller}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3812   \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{5261         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5262           lastIsNan = \textcolor{keyword}{false};}
\DoxyCodeLine{5263       \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5264         lastIsNan = \textcolor{keyword}{true};}
\DoxyCodeLine{5265       ++i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5266     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5267   \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5268     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} segmentStart = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5269     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5270     \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} lineDataSize = lineData.size();}
\DoxyCodeLine{5271     \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (i < lineDataSize) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5272       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (qIsNaN(lineData.at(i).y()) || qIsNaN(lineData.at(i).x()) ||}
\DoxyCodeLine{5273           qIsInf(}
\DoxyCodeLine{5274               lineData.at(i).y()))  \textcolor{comment}{// NaNs create a gap in the line. Also}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5275                                     \textcolor{comment}{// filter Infs which make drawPolyline block}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5276       \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5277         painter-\/>drawPolyline(}
\DoxyCodeLine{5278             lineData.constData() + segmentStart,}
\DoxyCodeLine{5279             i -\/ segmentStart);  \textcolor{comment}{// i, because we don't want to include the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5280                                 \textcolor{comment}{// current NaN point}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5281         segmentStart = i + 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5282       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5283       ++i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5284     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5285     \textcolor{comment}{// draw last segment:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5286     painter-\/>drawPolyline(lineData.constData() + segmentStart,}
\DoxyCodeLine{5287                           lineDataSize -\/ segmentStart);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5288   \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5289 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5290 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5291 \textcolor{comment}{/* end of 'src/plottable1d.h' */}}
